                  </div>
                  
                  <div class="paragraph-element">The reversible insertion reactions of the alkali cations A into NaMnFe(CN)<sub>6</sub> and relative insertion energy are as follows:

                     <div class="inline-equation" id="advs9580-disp-0003"><span class="inline-equation__construct"><!--FIGURE-->
                           <span class="fallback__mathEquation" data-altimg="/cms/asset/ba4f4466-d083-4f7c-9fdf-0deb2096df5e/advs9580-math-0003.png"></span><math altimg="urn:x-wiley:21983844:media:advs9580:advs9580-math-0003" display="block" location="graphic/advs9580-math-0003.png">
                              <semantics>
                                 <mtable displaystyle="true">
                                    <mtr>
                                       <mtd columnalign="right">
                                          <mrow>
                                             <mi>NaMnFe</mi>
                                             <msub>
                                                <mfenced close=")" open="(">
                                                   <mi>CN</mi>
                                                </mfenced>
                                                <mn>6</mn>
                                             </msub>
                                          </mrow>
                                       </mtd>
                                       <mtd>
                                          <mo>+</mo>
                                       </mtd>
                                       <mtd columnalign="left">
                                          <mrow>
                                             <mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi>
                                             <mo>→</mo>
                                             <mi>ANaMnFe</mi>
                                             <msub>
                                                <mfenced close=")" open="(">
                                                   <mi>CN</mi>
                                                </mfenced>
                                                <mn>6</mn>
                                             </msub>
                                             <mo>,</mo>
                                             <msub>
                                                <mi>E</mi>
                                                <mrow>
                                                   <mi>i</mi>
                                                   <mn>2</mn>
                                                </mrow>
                                             </msub>
                                             <mo linebreak="goodbreak">=</mo>
                                             <mi>E</mi>
                                             <mfenced close="]" open="[" separators="">
                                                <mrow>
                                                   <mi>ANaMnFe</mi>
                                                   <mfenced close=")" open="(">
                                                      <mi>CN</mi>
                                                   </mfenced>
                                                </mrow>
                                             </mfenced>
                                          </mrow>
                                       </mtd>
                                    </mtr>
                                    <mtr>
                                       <mtd></mtd>
                                       <mtd>
                                          <mo linebreak="newline">−</mo>
                                       </mtd>
                                       <mtd columnalign="left">
                                          <mrow>
                                             <mi>E</mi>
                                             <mfenced close="]" open="[" separators="">
                                                <mrow>
                                                   <mi>NaMnFe</mi>
                                                   <msub>
                                                      <mfenced close=")" open="(">
                                                         <mi>CN</mi>
                                                      </mfenced>
                                                      <mn>6</mn>
                                                   </msub>
                                                </mrow>
                                             </mfenced>
                                             <mo linebreak="badbreak">−</mo>
                                             <mi>E</mi>
                                             <mfenced close="]" open="[">
                                                <mi mathvariant="normal">A</mi>
                                             </mfenced>
                                          </mrow>
                                       </mtd>
                                    </mtr>
                                 </mtable>
                                 <annotation encoding="application/x-tex">$$\begin{eqnarray}{\mathrm{NaMnFe}}{{\left( {{\mathrm{CN}}} \right)}_6} &amp;+&amp; {\mathrm{A}} \to {\mathrm{ANaMnFe}}{{\left( {{\mathrm{CN}}} \right)}_6}, {{E}_{i2}} = E\left[ {{\mathrm{ANaMnFe}}\left( {{\mathrm{CN}}} \right)} \right]\nonumber\\ &amp;-&amp; E\left[ {{\mathrm{NaMnFe}}{{{\left( {{\mathrm{CN}}} \right)}}_6}} \right] - E\left[ {\mathrm{A}} \right] \end{eqnarray}$$</annotation>
                              </semantics></math></span><span class="inline-equation__label">(3)</span></div>where <i>E</i>[AMnFe(CN)<sub>6</sub>], <i>E</i>[NaMnFe(CN)<sub>6</sub>], <i>E</i>[ANaMnFe(CN)<sub>6</sub>], <i>E</i>[MnFe(CN)<sub>6</sub>] and <i>E</i>[A] represent total energy of AMnFe(CN)<sub>6</sub>, NaMnFe(CM)<sub>6</sub>, ANaMnFe(CN)<sub>6</sub>, MnFe(CN)<sub>6</sub> and metallic A calculated using DFT. The calculated energy of Na, Mg, K, and Ca atom are ‒1.30&nbsp;eV, ‒1.38&nbsp;eV, ‒1.02&nbsp;eV, and ‒1.92&nbsp;eV, respectively. The framework structure is fully optimized before use.<sup>[</sup><span><sup><a href="#advs9580-bib-0063" class="bibLink tab-link" id="advs9580-bib-0063_R_d190594207e2424" data-tab="pane-pcw-references" aria-label="Reference 63 - J. Mater. Chem. A">63</a></sup></span><sup>]</sup></div>
                  
                  <p>The minimum energy path way search of ion migration was conducted with the climbing image nudged elastic band (CI-NEB) method. The ions force convergence and the electronic energy convergence criteria were set to 0.05&nbsp;eV Å<sup>‒1</sup> and 10<sup>−7</sup>&nbsp;eV.<sup>[</sup><span><sup><a href="#advs9580-bib-0021" class="bibLink tab-link" id="advs9580-bib-0021_R_d190594207e2435" data-tab="pane-pcw-references" aria-label="Reference 21 - Energy Storage Mater.">21</a>, <a href="#advs9580-bib-0064" class="bibLink tab-link" id="advs9580-bib-0064_R_d190594207e2435" data-tab="pane-pcw-references" aria-label="Reference 64 - J. Chem. Phys.">64</a></sup></span><sup>]</sup></p>
                  
                  <p>The electronic properties calculations were conducted on a fully geometry-optimized Na<sub>2</sub>MnFe(CN)<sub>6</sub> (Na-PB), K<sub>2</sub>MnFe(CN)<sub>6</sub> (K-PB) and MgMnFe(CN)<sub>6</sub> (Mg-PB) cells. The occupation sites of Na, K, and Mg atoms were based on the above calculation results of <i>E</i><sub>i1</sub>.</p>
                  </section>
               </section>
            </section>
         </section>
